      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 13th century BC
       </b>
       . During the period 1300 to 1201 BC there were 250
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 93 were
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Types" title="Solar eclipse">
        partial
       </a>
       , 86 were annular, 64 were total, and 7 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was four, occurring in 16 different years: 1300 BC, 1289 BC, 1285 BC, 1282 BC, 1278 BC, 1271 BC, 1260 BC, 1253 BC, 1249 BC, 1242 BC, 1231 BC, 1224 BC, 1220 BC, 1213 BC, 1210 BC, and 1202 BC. One month, December 1210 BC, had two eclipses.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div style="clear:both;">
      </div>
